## Cycle 3 вҖ” 2026-04-08 03:16:52 UTC

**Cycle 29 done.**

Branch 2.2 (JSONL distillation) вҖ” highest derivative.

**202503.jsonl** (8,433 Edward msgs, Mar 2025) вҶ’ 3 new micro-decisions appended to `dna_core.md`:

1. **MD-13 зӯ–з•Ҙе“ҒиіӘ=MFE/MAEГ—вҲҡN** вҖ” avg(MFE/ATR)/avg(MAE/ATR) Г— вҲҡtradenum; combines per-trade quality with statistical confidence; blocks small-sample overfitting
2. **MD-14 иЎҢжғ…дёҚе°ҚдёҚеј·еҒҡ** вҖ” wrong regime = no edge; accept tiny loss rather than forcing strategy into hostile market
3. **MD-15 еӨҡз©әеҲҮжҸӣ=жўқд»¶еҲҶйӣў** вҖ” cond_le/cond_se for regime, filter_le/filter_se for entry; four independent conditions; generalizes to any binary state machine

- **MD-33** е°ҫз«ҜеҸЈж•ёжңҖе°ҸеҢ– вҖ” trendжң«ж®өжҢҒеҖү=дҪҺEVпјӣиӯҳеҲҘе°ҫз«ҜдҝЎиҷҹеҫҢз«ӢеҲ»зё®еҸЈпјӣе°Ҹж§“жЎҝжҙ»йҒҺе°ҫз«ҜжүҚиғҪйҮҚй–ӢеӨ§
